msg:A great holiday and leisure hotel with complete facilities and an excellent location. The scenery along the river is beautiful and it is very close to Red Street. There is also a free shuttle bus that can take the hotel to Red Street, which is very unique. I called the hotel in advance for consultation. The front desk lady answered my questions and added me on WeChat. She sent me an introduction to the scenic spots in Yan'an. It was really considerate. I was really surprised when I checked in and entered the lobby. The decoration style has the characteristics of northern Shaanxi. The little Red Army in the lobby is lifelike. The room is clean and sanitary, the bed is very soft and very comfortable to lie on. The bathrobe is also very soft and not hard to wear. The bathroom shower is separate, and taking a bath and going to the toilet do not affect each other, which saves a little time. In winter, you can skate on the lake next to it, and you can see the night view of Red Street from the room at night, which is very nice.

rating:3.2
posted:Posted September 19, 2023
msg:Very bad five-star hotel. Our group of 6 stayed in 3 twin rooms for two days, the price was 620 yuan per night/room. After staying for one night, there was a sudden power outage on the second day. It stands to reason that a five-star hotel should have a backup power supply. Even if there is no backup power supply, at least the elevator cannot be powered off. Generally, the elevators in residential buildings in the community also have dual power supplies to ensure the safety of the elevators. We lived on the seventh floor. The power outage just after breakfast. We were going to Yangjialing and other scenic spots. We had to climb to the seventh floor to get the things we went out. The six of us were all over 70 years old. The oldest was 84 years old and was already out of breath after climbing to the seventh floor. When we came back in the afternoon, the power still didn't come back. Fortunately, the hotel had to move us to the Wanda-managed Jiahua Hotel. This hotel has its own power supply and there was no power outage. I was quite satisfied after checking in. I didn't expect that there was a room 325 that was sweating in the middle of the night, and then I found that the air conditioner was not cooling. I didn't want to disturb the waiter in the middle of the night, so I had to open the balcony door to barely get through the night. I got up at 7:30 in the morning to have breakfast, but there was nothing left. Many containers on the dining table were empty. I had no choice but to fill my stomach and hurriedly left Yan'an and returned to Xi'an. This was the worst experience in a five-star hotel.

Hardware: newly renovated hotel, 4 star standard, good hardware, TV supports mobile phone screen projection
[Toilet]: Separate dry and wet, hot water is very comfortable, the matching toiletries should be customized by Wanda, not bad
[Service]: This is the most pleasant surprise. We just finished the reservation on the same day, and a 1V1 butler contacted us. Special thanks to Mia for showing us the way, preparing welcome fruits, and driving a battery car to take us to the Red Street. The service completely exceeded expectations.
[Breakfast]: At first I was worried that the breakfast in the newly opened hotel was not rich enough. Later I found that it was completely unnecessary. It may be due to the off-season. The diners are good, fruits, snacks, and pasta are good. I especially recommend the special "Jujube Pie" 😋

Because the room still smelled of decoration not long after the opening, the intimate Mia sent us a purifier. Adults can basically feel indifferent and sleep very well. If you are traveling with a baby, you still have to consider the smell of the baby. Sensitivity of ~

msg:比較少寫點評，出差會視情況選擇萬達酒店。這次入住衹是覺得和萬達的標準相差一些。酒店剛開業一個月，前台的表現並不是很萬達，很熱情，但是差點專業水準。房間很標準，裝修風格很喜歡，但是衞生情況不敢認同，可以見以下一些圖片，不管是是用料問題還是裝修問題，感覺臟臟的。但是床，沙發，地毯都很乾凈。淋浴房的下水有問題，才開業一月不到的新酒店，下水不暢，之後怎麼辦。窗户紗窗拉不上，最後我也放棄了。窗户外面酒店平台上，還留存着工人的鞋子，包括外枱麪很不乾淨，也許是才開業，沒來得及打掃。但是這個也不應該是萬達酒店的標準。酒店自助餐廳晚餐，門口銷售姑娘接待心不在焉，我果斷放棄與其溝通，換了一個銷售，問餐食和座位，告知沒有座位了，全滿了。給了很多其它就餐場所的建議。很熱情。但從另一個方面反應培訓不到位，或者職業素質有差。另外門口迎賓很熱情，主動幫助安排通勤車輛等。硬件到位，軟件差些意思，不知下次入住如何，很好的的大環境，在老區有這樣的酒店，還是願越來越好。

msg:槽點太多，簡單説幾點吧。1，房間空調温度感應器有問題，必須把空調温度設定在10度以下，才會出常温風，因為酒店的空調基本上是關的，我們連着幾個房間都是，2，房間的外玻璃麪全是泥，再好的湖景房都不好使，3，擺渡車不等個15分鐘以上別指望能坐到，給你的答覆永遠是催過了，4，餐廳的早餐簡單到極致，別指望吃到啥特色，能吃飽就錯了，另外你有錢都吃不到中餐和晚餐，因為它不供應。。。。。
